申報本埠增刊　汽車專刊

紐約汽車展覽會前夕 221

— 聶宇

一九三七年新模型全部陳列　空庭式拖車首次在會塲展覽　福特通用克雷斯勒另外舉行

紐約特訊（十一月八日）規模增鉅。陳列範圍擴大。抱有明年汽車事業鉅大希望之第三十七屆全國汽車展覽會。將於本星期三。歐洲休戰和平紀念日。下午二時。在此間四十六條與四十七條街間。蘭心登愛文義之太中央宮舉行。會期連接共八日。至十一月十八日晚十一時閉幕。

紐約車展會徽 222

本屆年會之展覽時間。較前稍有變更。星期日將照常開放。時間自中午至夜十時半。在星期中之第三日開幕。亦開前此未有之新例。已往各屆展覽會。通常於星期六日開幕。至下週之同日閉幕。此次展覽時間。除開幕日及星期日外。每日自上午十時半至夜十一時爲止

在十一月中舉行車展。本年係屬第二决。以十一月替代正月。此法係於去年間實行。其目的在增進汽車業中僱員工作之穩定。及吸引顧客於秋季購車。據稱去年於此兩項頗見成效。故主持展覽之汽車製造商聯合會决更以十一月爲本屆展覽之期。若輩挾一九三七年型之新車以俱來。其所希望之市塲。當能立刻映現於眼前。爲自一九二九年以來所未有云。

客車之參加展覽者。將代表二十家美國車廠牌子。及五家美國車廠牌子。總計全部汽車及底　約二百餘件。此外又有各種汽車零伴飾物等同時陳列。運貨汽車之展覽者將有七種牌號。參加展覽之美製汽車。計有別克·卡迪拉克·雪佛蘭·克雷斯勒·考特·第沙多·道琪·杜森堡·葛　亨·赫特森·拉薩爾·納許、拉飛埃脫·哇爾特斯摩別爾·派卡·披斯亞羅·潑萊茅斯·寳塔克·司蒂倍克·透拉平·及惠萊士。英製者爲亞薩士·奧斯汀·愛斯愛斯·傑瓜·愛姆琪·及拉共達。

拖車參加展覽本屆車展中將有拖車作首决之參加。其種類聞極衆多。中央宮之四層樓全部地位已劃作爲陳列之用。名廠之參加者約有二十四五家。所有各種　車輪上之家庭」將分別陳列。　模型不下五十餘種。此項陳列品預計將吸引一種特殊階級。尤其對於醉心遊遷生活或旅行生活之覜衆。將感極大興趣。拖車生活現方興未艾。汽車業中人預料其業務範圍將不下數千百萬元。

會期中有一日定爲國際日」。頗饒意義。爲本屆展覽之特色。央製汽車之參加實爲先聲。德國·瑞典。及法蘭西等國。亦已决派正式代表參予盛會。個人方面如英國·荷蘭·及瑞士等。凡與汽車車業有關者。亦均將到會。且已分別由各該國起程。

十一月十二日卽星期四。汽車製造商聯會之交通安全委會。將在康穆杜旅館舉行歡宴。屆時從事汽車安全之各領袖。將商討今後車輛安全之方。汽車工程師協會之常年宴會亦在同晚舉行。

福特林肯展覽一九三七年型之福特與林肯車。將不參加全國車展。但除在百老匯一，七一〇號之福特總銷售處陳列外。可於阿斯多旅館及花園衖兩處參觀之。此兩處之展覽期間亦與全國車展相同自星期三中午起至十八晚止。阿斯多旅館之跳舞廳及其毘連之玫瑰及勞萊爾兩屋。業已在梯格氏指導之下從事佈置。其色調係採取秋季之橙黃及古銅色等。福特V八式之各種車身。及林肯賽飛等車將於跳舞廳中陳列。巨型林肯V十二式及林肯賽飛等。將分別展覽於玫瑰及勞萊爾兩屋中。福特V八式運貨車之陳列處爲跳舞廳之中層擱樓。

阿斯多旅館之大跳舞廳中。除各種新車外。尙有其他有興味之模型陳列其中一組表示福特V八式全鋼車身及「中央平衡」式底盤等之重要特色。其所謂「經濟展覽」之中。包括有一架福特兩元倒射式化油機之巨大活動模型。一架「年紅燈」引擎表示其活動之循環方式。及引擎動作時之燃油經濟能力。另一陳列爲表示福特汽車之安全特色。關於「舒適與美觀」一點之陳列。將利用一輛白色之華麗式轎車。剖分爲二。以便審視。

通用汽車陳列會通用汽車公司亦將於華爾道夫亞斯多麗亞旅館中舉行新車陳列會。其時期一如全國車展。共爲八日。其會塲將佔旅館中之三層樓全部。塲中飾桑揕及白色。佈置甚爲新頴。另以緞光色之不銹鋼爲鑲飾。通用各種汽——雪佛蘭。寳搭克。哇特斯摩別爾。別克。拉薩爾。及卡迪拉克——將爲陳列中之主要特色。其他關於通用公司各方面之活動。及有關一般之汽車者。亦將分別展覽焉。

跳舞廳之中央爲四面式之環圓牆。由半透明式漆料所造。高三十尺之塔柱放光照耀。塔基裝以巨大之特製玻鏡。中望可見各車之「交通動態」。預料會場中展覽品之最能吸引觀衆者。當推一輛「剖分而二」之汽車。將陳列於廳事中最顯著之地方。此「劈分之汽車」係屬自働管理。據稱將初决以近代汽車動作中之直斷面顯示於衆。此項將汽車直剖爲二之工作。爲通用實騐工塲中之一種成功工程。其所需之時間將沂數個月云。飛休車身將展覽其新式之「整鋼塔尖式車身一。此爲一九三七年型通用各車之標凖裝置。

通用車展之研究部將陳列爲「車輪上之起居室」。共目的在表示通用汽車與。般家庭之舒適各點。一九三七年型汽車中之標準座位。可更變爲實用之沙發。其他近代汽車中之起居室零件爲火爐。無綫電。烟灰缸。車燈。等。可佈置成一完美之家庭。

會期中每日下午由卡爾好夫氏　之無綫電歌舞團奏演。以娛來賓。

克雷斯勒車展克雷斯勒萬國車展業已於昨日開幕。會塲在克雷斯勒大厦之一二層樓。預料此數日內往觀者必衆。此番陳列之主要出品爲潑萊茅斯。道琪。第沙多。及克雷斯勒。會塲佈置頗稱特色。如旋轉式展覽。及所裝之不見玻璃等。均爲前止所未有。燈光佈置亦極新頴。並有冬夏季空氣調節之展覽等。會塲中並另闢一室。專映關於該公司之出品電影。福特。通用。及克雷斯勒。三處展覽均不收費。全國車展之入場資爲晚六時前美金五角半。六時後七角半。票捐在內。

新超越式的　長途公共汽車 223

— 摩

乘坐舒適機力增大

火車的運輸業務。尤其是客運。近來有許多地方已被行駛長途的公共汽車侵入。因之象美國的幾家鐵道公司。在今年夏季裏。曾經拿低减客運費等來號召。同時在設備方面。也竭力改善。如採用流錢型車輛。地塞爾式引擎。和增加冷熱氣的空氣調節等。這都是一種吸引客運的手法。而在公共汽車公司方面呢。也决不示弱。向來祗以票價和便利上面來爭勝的。現在也更變方針。竭力在設備。速率，和舒適等處。大做工夫。我們祗要看美國長途客運汽車業中巨擘之一的「獵犬」綫的「超趨式客車」。就可以明瞭長途汽車的進步。已是十分的長足了。

這　近代　的「趟越式客車」是通用公司所承造的·在外表上和舊式長途汽車頗爲不同·車頭部並不尖銳·引擎的一部份業已袪除·所以樣子非常別緻·全身的流綫型保持着中庸的式子。並不過大·呌人一望上去·就有一個機力彌漫。結構堅實。和輕快流麗的印象。第一批的新車計共三百二十五輛。

車身的外面因爲採用金屬物爲飾。燦爛奪目。異常新頴可喜。車頭部因爲後引擎的緣故。所以從橡皮製的保險槓以上。直到車頂僞止。始漸漸地平斜向後。很爲好看。駕駛人的坐位。正在車子的前端。位置很高。足以淸晰地瞭望來車。和前面的路上情形。比起舊式汽車確要高明多多。這是由於他的地拉優越。和保險玻璃的大風屛的綠故。

乘客的地位也大爲增高。在震搖錢以上。聲息和塵埃多能避免不少。旅客們從保不破碎的窗玻璃中。可以瞭望來往客車的車頂。在舒適方面說。因爲將「輪上坐位」完全取銷。所有的座位一槪舒適。車軸和車輪的震動。就不致擾及乘客了。

雖然乘客的座位提高。但是全車的重心却較前大爲抑低。這樣一來。在安全和載物方面。獲得格外的利便。車身全部的高矗部份也已銷除。車中的坐椅。墊子非常厚軟。椅架係用鎂及鋁的金屬物所造。十分悅目。坐墊深軟。頭部靠依是一種科學的設計。並且有可移動的臂靠。坐椅可自由改換位置。共有四種不同的位置。供客自擇。可以望野境，讀書報，休息，或瞌睡。身子高而腿部長的乘客。他在車中也能獲得相當的舒適。因爲坐椅間的伸足部份。已較往昔增加了不少呢。

車中搭客們的伸足地位雖然增寬。可是全車的地位同時增大。這種「超越式客車」中可搭客三十六人。從前不過二十三人而已。這個較多的地位。是由於將車廂伸展至原來的摩托地位而獲得的。車廂中寬暢無阻。一些沒有障礙物。因爲許多隨手携帶的行李。都置放在下層的車廂中。與客坐截然隔雖。就格外見到暢適。座椅的上面另裝一些櫃架。專備客人們放置零星包紮物件等之用。客人們從平地登車。祗要一舉足之勞。就是一個凹嵌在內通廊。與全車的長度相同。座位處却在這通廊的上一步。車廊內部完全近代化，光亮噴漆的板壁。鑲以金屬物邊綠。燈光也安全採用新式。車項用摩沙玻璃爲飾。燈光由內部照出。柔和而華麗。別有風趣。

「超越式客車」的引擎力量非常鉅大。裝在車的尾部。與後軸並行。這樣裝法。不但增進機力和效用。並具在聲息行動方面。格外的安靜平穩。震動减少。熄滅時氣息也引擎所在地與客坐的車廂。分別隔離。甚爲嚴密。故震動較少。車底層有兩個車廂。建造十分嚴密。水和灰塵一些也不會侵入。這裏專爲安置衣箱行李箱籠及大件包裹之用。原來公共汽車中常見的車項包裹架子。已經完全取消了。存放行李的車間。有門直向外面開啟。可以隨便放入或取出。車子行駛的時候。門是完全封閉的。這種新車子的行李運輸量比較從前舊式的要增加不少。新車全部大半爲堅緻的鋁金屬所造。所以結構上的力量很是偉大可以增多兩噸的重量呢。

海外汽車談片 224

— 愚

美國電影明星購置派卡派卡車雍容華貴。向爲有產階級所樂用，近據美國加利福尼亞派卡汽車銷售商阿桑納氏之調査。在美國之著名電影明星中。其已購置派卡汽車者。在一百人以上。據桑氏稱。好萊塢爲各種漂亮及新式事物之集中所。特開風氣之先。爲各方觀瞻所繫。市上大號派卡及一二〇號型所在都是。足令外來人士。心嚮往之。尤其在著名影星導演等之集合塲所。派卡更爲一時領袖汽車。桑氏又稱好萊塢事物除漂亮之外。又必具有實用及需用之要素。派卡之風格精絕。能與影星相得益彰云云。

車上無綫電收音機　美國之無綫電事業日益發達。據估計本年上半年中之收音機銷數。已超過一九三五年之最高峯。生產方面多出百分之十五至二十五。銷路上漲起百分之十五至三十。其中允以汽車中裝置無綫電收音機者爲更見增進。本年一月至六月份止之六個月中。無綫電收音機之用於車上者。其銷數超出一九三五年自百分之三十至一百五十。一九三五年末汽車之裝有無綫電機註册者祗佔百分之十七。其數目爲客車三·九〇〇·〇〇〇輛。而據估計至本年底止。其數將達五·〇〇〇·〇〇〇輛云。

有興趣的汽車分析　據美國汽車會一一九三六年發行之「汽車事實與數字」一書一內稱。一九三五年美國所製造之汽車與零件等。其批發之總價值為美金三，三一九，九七三元。去年美國所造之汽車其數量爲四，一一九，八一一輛。與汽車製造銷售等直接或問接上所僱用之員工。其總數逾六，六〇〇，〇〇〇人，其中四三九，〇〇〇人。係直接受僱於汽車及其零伴之製造。若輩於一九三五年間所得之工資數爲六五七，三三二，〇〇〇元。一九三五年所產之汽車數量。及其銷售上所得之價値。較之汽車事業最不景氣之一九三二年高出幾達百分之二〇〇。以磅數及馬力計算一九三五年汽車之價値。其結果如下。一九三五年汽車每磅價格平鈞爲美金二角一分。較之一九三五年汽車每磅價格平均爲美金二角一分。較之一九二五年出品廉去一角七分。以馬力計則去年汽車每匹馬力之售價爲美金七元。一九二五年時則爲二十七元五角。

啟事　亞，愚，振民，敷，三原，摩，凌雲，諸君鑒。十一月份汽車增刋稿費。現已結淸。請於每月六日至十日。及十六日至二十日止。具條蓋章。向會計處領取爲荷。　汽車增刋編輯部啟。

1936.12.09

Bandit-Puppet Conspiracy to Attack Xinghe, Decided to Reinforce Troops at Nanhao Trenches, Rehe Puppet Troops Departed from West of Dolon, Large Quantities of Military Supplies Transported to Zhangbei, Wang Ying's Bandit Troops Deserted in Succession, Northern Sui War Expected to End Soon 1

(Zhangjiakou) A certain side, due to repeated bandit-puppet determination to counterattack, all failed, decided to reinforce troops at Nanhao trenches, fiercely attack Xinghe in Eastern Sui, plotting to occupy Jining and cut off the Ping-Sui Railway traffic. According to information from a certain special agency in Jiabusi, bandit-puppets are no longer allowed to suffer defeats. If necessary, Rehe troops will be used as the main force to attack Sui. On the 7th, more than ten commanders of a certain side arrived in Zhangbei from the temple, and immediately went to the Nanhao trenches. There are currently 3,000 Rehe troops concentrated on the earth and stone roads in Zhangbei County, who will join the 6,000 Rehe troops of a certain side originally stationed in Nanhao trenches to invade Xinghe. On the 8th, more than ten carts of sacks and military supplies were transported from Zhangbei to Nanhao trenches. Zhang Wanqing's troops immediately supervised laborers to stack the sacks into fortifications. 5,000 regular troops and Rehe troops of a certain side were stationed in Kangbao, Baochang, and the Yulinggou Gaoshanbao area of Guyuan County on the 8th. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) Most of Wang Ying's bandit troops have surrendered, Wang only escaped with his life. The military affairs in Northern Sui are expected to end. It is anticipated that the remaining bandits will be eliminated and the surrendered troops will be reorganized, which can be completed within a few days. Northern Sui will soon be at peace. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) Shi Yushan, brigade commander of Wang Ying's troops, has revolted and is scheduled to come to Sui on the 9th to meet with General Fu Zuoyi. Shi sent a telegram to Sui on the 8th announcing his revolt. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) Wang Ying sent his chief of staff, Kou Ziyan, to Sui on the 8th to negotiate the surrender. Kou has now left Sui. Pan and Wang returned to Wulanhua on the 8th. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Jining Telegram: A certain country's instructors of the puppet Meng troops in Chahar North recently held a meeting in Shangdu, with important discussions. Various guilds and chambers of commerce in Shangdu were ordered to prepare tens of thousands of catties of cakes. All civilian houses are affixed with slips stating "Occupied by a certain army and a certain division." A large army will pass through within days. More than 3,000 puppet cavalry are active between Dolon and Pangjiang, seemingly intending to turn to Western Sui to harass. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Jining Telegram: Military News: (1) The puppet Jin-Cheng Railway has stopped passenger and freight transportation, transporting puppet troops westward day and night. (2) A large batch of poisonous gas has recently been transported to Dolon and Chahar North and stored in Jiabusi, Shangdu and other places for future use. (3) Many more puppet troops have arrived in Huluyu, Baochang. (8th Telegram)

(Beiping) Suiyuan Telegram: The remaining bandits in Bailingmiao have been eliminated. A certain side in Eastern Sui is actively preparing for war. According to surrendered puppet bandits, there are 10,000 puppet troops in Shangdu, including a part of a certain country's soldiers, more than 30 airplanes, and more than 20 tanks. Because a certain side does not trust the puppet bandits, these military equipment are all driven by people from a certain country. Once the equipment is ready, they will launch a large-scale invasion. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Jining Telegram: Because of the severe cold in Mongolia and Suiyuan, which is not conducive to marching, the a certain army headquarters outside the Pass has changed its plan of invading Suiyuan. It intends to launch a large-scale invasion after the winter solstice. The deployment of the puppet Mongolian army will focus on defense, with the aim of not losing Shangdu, Damiao, and Jiabusi. The commando will take harassment as their goal, aiming at Wuchuan, Bailingmiao, Taolin, and Xinghe. It is predicted that there will be no major battles before the new year. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) The puppet troops of Wu Guiting and others from Rehe and Chahar, totaling five regiments, are now concentrated around Zhangbei. There were no changes in Eastern Sui on the 8th. Wang Ying's bandit troops, totaling six regiments, revolted at 2:00 PM on the 8th, detouring to Wulanhua in Wuchuan County. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) A Wang met with Fu Zuoyi in Sui to discuss important public matters. He went to Baotou at noon on the 8th and will return to Hangjin Banner. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) The current situation in Eastern Sui is peaceful. The situation in Sui-Bao, according to news obtained on the 8th, is as follows: (1) Wang Ying's bandit troops are currently rebelling. Among them, the leader's party has arrived at [illegible], negotiating the aftermath with Zeng Yanyi. Wang himself only led a few hundred people to flee, and our army is in pursuit. The reward of 30,000 yuan has greatly boosted morale. The exact number of Wang's troops who have revolted will be known on the 9th. (2) On the morning of the 8th, eight bandit planes bombed the Iolanhua town area of Wuchuan County. Our military and civilians defended well and suffered no losses. (3) Captured bandits confessed that Lei Zhongtian, the commander of the bandit-puppet division who launched the counterattack on Bailingmiao, is missing. On the 8th, Fu Zuoyi telegraphed the troops stationed in the temple to inspect the corpses of bandit soldiers who died around the temple, suspecting that Lei had died in the chaotic army. Lei's entire division has rebelled. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Guihua) The Mongol-puppet bandits attempting to invade Eastern Sui are still actively transporting large quantities of military supplies to Zhangbei and Shangdu. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Guihua) The Sui Provincial Government issued a notice on the 7th, stating in brief: During military operations, the people should prepare houses, boil water, and do their best to collect food, fodder for mules and horses, firewood, charcoal, and other items for temporary use at the stations where the troops stay and in the villages and towns where they reside. The troops should be especially peaceful to the people of each village. Since they are providing cash provisions, they should pay the price accordingly. If cash payment is inconvenient at the moment, a formal receipt should be signed and issued by the highest local official to the township head or village guide, who will forward it to the Provincial Government for deduction and reimbursement. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Guihua) Fu Zuoyi hosted a banquet on the evening of the 8th for student representatives from Ping, Tianjin, Shanghai, and Shaanxi who came to Sui to comfort the officers and soldiers. A total of more than twenty people attended. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Yan Xishan Reports on the Battle Situation at the Front Lines 2

(Nanjing) Yan Xishan telegraphed Zhao Pilian to forward to relevant parties in the capital, reporting on the battle situation. The original telegram briefly stated: According to Chairman Fu's telegram, Wang Ying led more than 1,500 cavalry bandits, fleeing from Hala Yili Geng, Yisheng Yong, about 70-80 li west of Wulanhua and other places, towards Xilamuleng (i.e. Damiao). The remaining bandit troops who attacked Bailingmiao this time have fled to Xilamuleng, Hayue Temple, 120 li northwest of the Fourth Prince's Mansion, and other places. A certain cavalry division has been dispatched to encircle and suppress them. Zhao Pilian told reporters on the 8th that the front lines in Sui province have been quiet recently. The National Army is now defending tightly, and if the bandits come to invade, it will be difficult for them to succeed. Regarding De Wang's situation, there have been few letters and telegrams to the capital recently, so the details are unknown. The central government's disposition of the Mengzheng Council in Chahar will have to wait for the decision of the Executive Yuan. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Japanese Military Exercises 3

(Tianjin) The mechanized chemical warfare team of the 2nd Infantry Regiment of the Tianjin Japanese Army and the 14th Destroyer Squadron held a siege and defense battle of the seaport and the outskirts of Tianjin. Preparations began on the 8th, starting at 9:00 AM on the 9th. The exercise grounds in the morning were in the lower reaches of the Hai River, Chengtangzhuang, Salty Water Dagu, and Tanggu. The infantry of the two battalions of the Tangshan Pinbu and Kagawa all joined. Rest at noon. The exercises continued at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, with rest at 5:00 PM in the afternoon. Night combat exercises at 8:00 PM, ending at 10:00 PM. Tashiro intends to lead his staff to the position for inspection. Mutaaguchi, commander of the 1st Regiment stationed in Beiping, accompanied by his subordinates, the two battalions of Matsuyama and Nishie, came to watch the battle on the 8th. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Japanese cavalry plans to conduct field exercises in the southern Tianjin countryside in Caijiatai, Zhiyuan Tou, and Xinjiayuan from the 16th to the 19th. On the 8th, Lieutenant Araki was dispatched to occupy more than 100 civilian houses in various villages. (8th Special Dispatch)

Qingdao Incident is About to be Resolved, Both Sides' Opinions are Gradually Approaching, Japanese Marines to Withdraw Within Days 4

(Qingdao) After several negotiations between Shen Honglie and the Japanese Consul Nishihiko over the Qingdao Incident, the opinions of both sides are now gradually approaching. There is news that the Japanese Marines will withdraw within days. The situation in the city and the Sifang Cangkou area has eased compared to before. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Personnel from the Japanese Navy, Army, and foreign affairs-related departments in Qingdao held a meeting on the 8th to discuss the results of the Shen-Nishi talks. In addition, in order to resolve the Qingdao Incident as soon as possible, Shen held a fifth meeting with Consul Nishi again on the evening of the 8th. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) The newly appointed Commander Hasegawa of the Japanese 3rd Fleet arrived in Qingdao on the 8th aboard the "Asatsuki" destroyer. He landed with Oikawa in the afternoon and officially took over at the Grand Hotel. Oikawa is scheduled to return to Japan by ship on the 9th. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) A certain central figure and this side have both telegraphed Shen, advocating a peaceful resolution of the Qingdao issue under the principle of not harming sovereignty. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The two destroyers of the 14th Destroyer Squadron, "Kiku" and "Hagi", sailed to Qingdao in the morning to stand guard, in addition to the Marines who landed on the 8th to stay in Tanggu and participate in the land and naval exercises. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) When Mayor Shen Honglie and Japanese Consul Nishi Chun met here, Shen considered the demands made by the Japanese side to be "unreasonable" and firmly rejected them. Although the nature of these demands has not been announced locally, it is widely believed that they will not go beyond the scope of the five demands mentioned in the telegram from Tokyo. It is said that although the progress of the negotiations between the two sides is not good, the tense atmosphere has eased. (8th Reuters Telegram)

(Jinan) Japanese military attache Ishino, stationed in Jinan, returned from Qingdao and spoke about the Qingdao situation, saying that it was peaceful but not yet resolved. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Guo Binghe, head of the Qingdao Finance Bureau, was ordered by Shen today to go to Jinan to meet with Han and report on the Qingdao situation. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Jinan) Yesterday, Ishino went to Qingdao, got off the train in Cangkou, and wanted to inspect the works, but our side refused and sent someone to accompany him in a car to Qingdao. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Consul General Nishi, Naval Attache Tajiri, Army Attache Yahagi, and others met with Commander Oikawa on the "Izumo" warship at 9:30 this morning, and then held a meeting with Oikawa's staff. Army Attache Ishino stationed in Jinan reported on the information from the Shandong Provincial Government. Consul General Nishi explained the progress of the talks with Mayor Shen and agreed on countermeasures. (8th Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Qingdao) Lieutenant General Hasegawa, the newly appointed commander of the 3rd Fleet, officially took over from Commander Oikawa on the "Izumo" warship at 1:00 PM today and immediately took office. Lieutenant General Oikawa left the ship and landed at 1:30 PM. All warships held a boarding ceremony and fired a 15-gun salute. (8th Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Qingdao) Lieutenant General Hasegawa, who took office as Commander of the 3rd Fleet today, issued a statement saying: "I have just assumed my duty as Commander of the 3rd Fleet to be responsible for the security of this area. Recently, a labor dispute occurred in a local yarn factory, and the dispute was ongoing. Fortunately, the city government's sincere attitude and the mediation of the Japanese parties concerned were successful, and it can be resolved within days, which is a cause for celebration for both countries." (8th Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Qingdao) Consul General Nishi met with Mayor Shen on the evening of the 7th and exchanged views. As a result, both sides agreed to cooperate in resolving the Qingdao Incident as soon as possible. (8th Domei News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) This capital received a telegram from Qingdao on the 8th, reporting that the situation in Qingdao City has eased slightly compared to before. Mayor Shen is still negotiating with the Japanese side. Judging from the current situation, if the other side is sincere, the matter may be resolved in the short term. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Information from the Japanese Embassy: Sino-Japanese Negotiations Have Not Broken Down, Suma to Visit Gao Zongwu Again Today 5

(Nanjing) According to news from the Japanese Embassy, the Sino-Japanese negotiations have not broken down and will continue to be reconciled. The rumor that Ambassador Kawagoe will return home for a trip is unlikely to be realized for the time being. According to a spokesman for the Japanese Embassy, Consul General Suma is scheduled to meet with Gao Zongwu, director of the Asian Department of our Foreign Ministry, at 3:00 PM tomorrow to continue exchanging opinions on Sino-Japanese diplomatic issues. The rumor that Sino-Japanese diplomatic negotiations have broken down and been interrupted is not accurate. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic circles, since Kawagoe left Beijing for Shanghai, our side's attitude and process on various negotiation issues between China and Japan have been reported in the newspapers. The bleak future of the current negotiations between the city and Japan is indeed a fact. However, after Ambassador Kawagoe left Beijing, the side negotiations of the diplomatic officials of both sides continued to exchange opinions. However, the two sides did not meet on the 8th. Under the current circumstances, whether the negotiations on adjusting relations between China and Japan can make progress will depend on how the Japanese side handles the Suiyuan and Qingdao incidents. Furthermore, the Qingdao incident seemed to have eased slightly yesterday. If the Japanese side can seek a solution in the right way, it is hoped that it will come to an end in the short term. Mayor Shen sent a telegram to the capital on the 8th to report. Foreign telegrams stated that Ambassador Kawagoe intends to return to Japan for a trip, but according to various sources, it seems that this will not be realized for the time being. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Tokyo) At noon on the 8th, the Seiyukai first visited the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister through Secretary-General Ando. After hearing the truth about the current state of Sino-Japanese negotiations, they expressed their beliefs and strongly criticized the government for its future policies. They also heard the current situation regarding general issues with the Soviet Union, Europe, and the United States, and advocated establishing a diplomatic national policy and promoting national diplomacy, which attracted attention from all aspects. (8th Domei News Agency Telegram)

Italy Denies Recognition of the Puppet State 6

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic circles, after a certain semi-official Italian news agency published a message stating that the Italian government would recognize "Manchukuo," the Ministry of Foreign Affairs copied the original text and questioned the Italian ambassador. On the morning of the 8th, the Italian Embassy sent Secretary Felaire to visit Li Dijun, Director of the Intelligence Department of the Foreign Ministry, saying that the Italian government had no such intention. The record was completely untrue and should be the responsibility of the news agency. It has also sent a letter to the news agency to make a clear correction to avoid misunderstandings. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to diplomatic circles, after Foreign Minister Zhang raised several questions with the Italian ambassador regarding the Italian-Japanese agreement, the Italian ambassador has cabled his home government for instructions. As of the 8th, he has not yet formally replied to our Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (8th Special Dispatch)

Sharp Competition Arises in Economic Interests between Japan and Germany 7

(Tokyo) According to news received by this newspaper today, the German government recently requested the Japanese commercial consul in Berlin to reduce Japan's exports to Germany, otherwise it would allow Germany to increase its exports to Japan, predicting that there will be fierce competition in the economic interests of the two countries. It is reported that the current trade agreement between the two countries stipulates that the ratio of Japan's annual exports to Germany to Germany's exports to Japan is one to four, but last year Japan's trade with Germany was actually in surplus, with a ratio of one to three to one to two, which is very different from the originally stipulated one to four, causing deep dissatisfaction on the German side. It is rumored that Japan is preparing to reject Germany's above-mentioned request on the pretext that Japan has indirectly purchased a large number of German machinery products dumped in China. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Ministry of Finance Continues to Allocate Bandit Suppression Funds to Jin and Sui 8

—500,000 Yuan—

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance, considering the urgency of bandit suppression in Suiyuan, had previously allocated 500,000 yuan in temporary funds, which were remitted to Jin for distribution. The approved increase of more than 190,000 yuan in regular military expenses for bandit suppression in Jin and Sui was also remitted starting last month. Now, after Zhao Pilian met with Finance Minister Kong in Shanghai and discussed the matter, another 500,000 yuan in temporary funds was allocated. The Executive Yuan has reviewed the budget for various bandit suppression items in Sui prepared by the Taiyuan Pacification Commissioner's Office through repeated deliberations by the military, political, and financial departments, and has already reached a result. In addition, the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan is scheduled to meet in September to review the 10 million yuan public bond issuance案 for Jin Province. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Shandong Security Forces Assist in Anti-Smuggling 9

(Tianjin) Smuggled goods from Tianjin are transported to northern Shandong via the Tianjin-Jinan Highway. Smuggling is rampant south of Leling. The Shandong Security Forces have specially formed a guerrilla team to assist the Dezhou Highway Smuggling Inspection Office in searching and blocking. (8th Special Dispatch)

Opening Up the Economy of North China, Japanese Funding is Difficult to Resolve, Li Sihao Meets Song to Report on the Progress of Negotiations 10

(Tianjin) Capital is still the prerequisite issue for the economic development of North China. Although the plan approved by the Tianjin Japanese military department to the central leadership has been approved, conflicts with Guanwai are becoming increasingly serious in terms of the political views held. The South Manchuria Railway Xingzhong Corporation is restricted by Guanwai forces and cannot directly invest. The various domestic financial groups are also taking a wait-and-see attitude due to the Suiyuan incident. The Tianjin military department continues to engage in endless superficial contacts, but in reality, they will all come to a standstill. The Tianjin-Shijiazhuang Railway and Longyan Mine affairs will also be difficult to organize due to the difficulty in finding capital. Staff Officer Wachi flew to Qingdao a few days ago to meet with Commander Oikawa of the fleet to discuss the Qingdao case, hoping not to expand it, so that North China can gradually return to stability and various plans can be implemented. Recently, observing the policy held by this side, the Qingdao case will take a sharp turn and can be resolved peacefully. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Li Sihao went to the Political Council in the morning of the 8th to meet with Song and report on the issue of economic development in North China discussed with Tashiro in Tianjin. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Imai went to the Political Council in the morning of the 8th to meet with Song for discussion. (8th Special Dispatch)

Comforting the Officers and Soldiers of Suiyuan 11

(Beiping) The Beiping Student Suiyuan War of Resistance Support Association held its second representative assembly on the afternoon of the 7th, passing the organizational outline of the war zone service group and the date of the members' assembly, and deciding on the use of donations raised by students from various schools. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Anqing) All circles in Wan'an organized a society to aid the officers and soldiers defending the territory, nominating 15 organizations including the provincial party department as executive members, and telegraphed comfort to the officers and soldiers at the front. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong All Circles Aid to Suiyuan Association decided on fundraising methods on the 8th, dividing them into three types: donations, voluntary contributions, and contributions of one day's income. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) All circles in Hong Kong held an aid to Suiyuan conference at the Tung Wah Hospital on the 8th, electing eight directors of fundraising and starting to raise funds separately. The Guangdong-Hong Kong First Aid Team decided to form a rescue team to go to Suiyuan. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications employees remitted more than 2,200 yuan in one day's salary to Sui on the 8th and telegraphed Fu to express their condolences. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) After arriving in Beiping, Liu Ruiheng left Beiping for Datong on the evening of the 8th to go to Suiyuan to inspect the first aid work at the front and visit Fu. (8th Special Dispatch)

Japan Plans to Take Luqing Salt to Produce Chemical Products 12

(Tianjin) The Japanese Salt Manufacturing Company plans to set up a salt manufacturing company in Tianjin and Qingdao respectively to take Luqing salt to produce chemical products for military use. The negotiations on the occupation of the Changlu Salt Pond and Salty Beach are still at an impasse. The Japanese side plans to assign it to the Xingzhong Corporation for use and plans to start construction of a food warehouse. (8th Special Dispatch)

Chairman Lin's Activities in Fujian 13

(Fuzhou) Chairman Lin summoned the design committee members of the provincial party department on the 7th to listen to reports on party affairs and commended them. Japanese Consul Uchida also went to the Office of the Chairman to pay his respects and extend his greetings, before departing after a 20-minute conversation. (8th Central News Agency Telegram)

Record of the Executive Yuan's Regular Meeting: Resolution to Request Commendation for Yan Xishan's Mother; Appointment of Zhao Dengyu and Li Xin as Committee Members of Hebei Province; Method of Conferring Honors and Compensation on Huang Fu Largely Agreed Upon 14

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held its 291st regular meeting on the morning of the 8th, attended by He Yingqin, Wu Dingchang, Chen Shuren, Wang Shijie, Wu Zhongxin, Zhang Jia'ao, Chen Shaokuan, and Chairman Zhang Qun.

Reported Matters: A memorandum from the Secretariat and the Department of Political Affairs stated that the Ministry of Interior had requested the compilation of centrally promulgated laws and regulations. Following the 288th resolution of the Yuan, the matter was submitted to the Department for drafting a method to be presented for approval. A method for compiling and printing a collection of centrally promulgated administrative laws and regulations was carefully prepared and submitted for review.

Matters for Discussion: (1) A joint report from Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries and Minister Jiang of the Ministry of Interior regarding the drafting of implementation measures based on the outline of the "Measures for Reorganizing Farmland Water Conservancy Along Rivers and Lakes," requested review and approval. The resolution was passed to approve both the draft implementation measures and the outline, and the Yuan would promulgate and instruct their implementation. (2) A report from Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries, and Acting Minister Yu Jue of the Ministry of Transportation, which was submitted for review, concerned the draft of the "Temporary Regulations for the Navigation Donation in the Huai River Basin" and the "Temporary Charter for the Huaiyin Sluice Management Office," as well as the "Temporary Measures for Levying Navigation Donations in the Huai River Basin." After consulting with the Huai River Commission and dispatching personnel for joint discussion, it was proposed to change the title of the original charter to "Temporary Charter for the Collection of Sluice Usage Fees in the Huai River Basin by the Ministry of Finance," and the title of the original measures to "Temporary Measures for the Collection of Sluice Usage Fees in the Huai River Basin by the Ministry of Finance." The articles were appropriately revised and implemented on a trial basis for six months. The revised charter and measures were submitted for review. The resolution was passed based on the review opinions. (3) A joint report from Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance, Minister Wu of the Ministry of Industries, and Acting Minister Yu Jue of the Ministry of Transportation requested modification of the "Regulations on Marking the Weight of Shipping Packages" to ensure the effective implementation of international conventions. A draft revision was submitted for approval and implementation. The resolution was passed for the Yuan to promulgate and implement. (4) Deputy Yuan Chief Kong proposed that the mother of Director Yan of the Taiyuan Pacification Commissioner's Office had donated a substantial amount of national currency, totaling 870,000 yuan, to support national salvation. He requested a public vote on how to specially commend her. The resolution was passed to request the National Government to issue a commendation order and award a gold medal in accordance with the "Measures for Rewarding People Who Donate Money for National Salvation." (5) The Ministries of Interior, Military Affairs, Finance, Industries, Education, Transportation, and Railways, as well as the Health Administration and the Relief Commission, reported that they had been instructed to review the "General Budget of Local Ordinary and Business Income and Expenditure for Shandong Province in the 25th Year." After consulting with the National Economic Council and dispatching personnel for joint discussion, ten points of opinion were drafted and submitted for review along with the review opinions. The resolution was passed based on the review opinions.

Appointments and Removals: The resolution was passed to remove Liang Jianzhang and Duan Zonglin, members of the Hebei Provincial Government, due to other assignments. Zhao Dengyu and Li Xin were appointed as members of the Hebei Provincial Government. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) National Government Committee Member and former Chairman of the Executive Yuan's Political Reorganization Committee stationed in Beiping, Huang Fu, passed away from illness at his residence in Shanghai. At the Executive Yuan's regular meeting on the 8th, the method of conferring honors and compensation was largely discussed as follows: (1) Hold a public funeral; (2) Submit a request to the National Government for a commendation order; (3) Allocate funds for funeral expenses. After telegraphically requesting instructions from the Yuan Chief, the matter will be submitted to the National Government for a decision. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) Regarding the Sino-British Gengkuan loan borrowed by the Huai River Commission for the construction of the Huaiyin, Shaobo, Liujian, and Gaoyou sluices, the original contract stipulated that the Ministry of Finance would guarantee it. The principal and interest repayment fund was also stipulated to be allocated from the revenue of navigation freight donations collected after the completion of the project. If it was insufficient, the Ministry of Finance, as the guarantor, would make up the difference. Because the Ministry of Finance bore the responsibility of unlimited guarantee for this loan, it established the "Collection Office for Sluice Usage Fees in the Huai River Basin Area" in accordance with the contract to collect usage fees. Su Nehou was appointed as the director of the office. The "Temporary Charter for the Collection Office" and the "Temporary Measures for Collecting Usage Fees" were also submitted to the Executive Yuan and passed at the meeting on the 8th. The rate and level of this usage fee are based on the product of the length and width of the ship's deck in meters, with one grade for every five meters. For passenger and cargo ships under five meters at the Huaiyin Sluice, the fee is one yuan per ship, and one yuan is added for every five meters. Empty ships are charged one-fourth of the fee for loaded ships. The Shaobo and Liujian Sluices charge three-tenths of the Huai rate for loaded ships, and one-third for fixed ships. The Gaoyou Sluice charges one-tenth of the Huai rate for loaded ships, and empty ships are exempt. This will be implemented on a trial basis for six months. If the future income exceeds the amount of principal and interest due, the donation rate should be appropriately reduced to ease the burden on boat owners. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) The draft implementation measures for the outline of the "Measures for Reorganizing Farmland Water Conservancy Along Rivers and Lakes" was passed by the Executive Yuan on the 8th. The main points are as follows: (1) The implementation of the "Measures for Reorganizing Farmland Water Conservancy Along Rivers and Lakes" shall be in accordance with the provisions of these implementation measures. (2) The boundaries of ordinary flood lines of rivers and lakes and the scope required for flood storage shall be jointly surveyed and determined by the provincial and municipal governments and the central water conservancy authorities. The standards are: A. For rivers and lakes where the fundamental treatment plan has been completed, the boundaries of arable land along the banks may be delineated and managed. B. Rivers and lakes that have been surveyed and have reliable hydrological records may be used to delineate the land along the banks, provided that it does not interfere with water conservancy, and reorganized in advance. C. Rivers and lakes that have not been surveyed should maintain the status quo for land that is flooded or stored, and reorganization should be postponed. (3) Any reclamation and cultivation in low-lying areas that had flood storage functions in the past, the construction of reservoirs upstream, or the widening of river channels downstream must be planned and approved in advance. For two or more provinces and cities, the plan must be submitted to the central government for approval. (4) After the demarcation of boundaries and the construction of dikes along rivers and lakes, the land between the dikes shall be operated by public farms established by the provincial and municipal governments. (5) Provincial and municipal governments should conduct a survey of the number of tenant farmers and owner-farmers, as well as the area of land, before operating public farms on the land between the dikes, and formulate detailed plans in accordance with the following regulations to be sent to the Ministries of Interior, Industries, and Finance for verification and record-keeping: A. The scope of the farm; B. The farm management organization; C. Business operations and implementation steps; D. Farmer organization and treatment; E. Water conservancy construction; F. Placement of surplus farmers; G. Budget; H. Profit distribution; I. Other. (6) Provincial and municipal governments should report the business conditions, revenue and expenditure budgets, and final accounts of the B-operated farms in the dike area to the Ministries of Interior, Industries, and Finance for record-keeping each business year. (7) Private land in the dike area shall be requisitioned by the provincial and municipal governments in accordance with the law. The compensation may be paid in the form of land price vouchers. Provincial and municipal governments should formulate detailed measures for issuing land price vouchers and submit them to the Ministries of Interior and Finance for forwarding to the Executive Yuan for approval and implementation. (8) Surplus farmers shall be re-organized by the provincial and municipal governments, and wasteland shall be delineated for them to reclaim. (9) The area of wasteland reclaimed by surplus farmers shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 193 of the Land Law, and the land price may be paid with land price vouchers. (10) The water conservancy in the areas reclaimed by surplus farmers shall be planned by the provincial and municipal governments on their behalf. (11) The migration expenses of surplus farmers shall be subsidized by the provincial and municipal governments. (12) If surplus farmers need subsidies for cattle production and living expenses during the period when the reclaimed wasteland has not been cultivated, they may borrow land price vouchers from the provincial and municipal governments. If there are no land price vouchers to borrow, the provincial and municipal governments shall provide loans as appropriate. The interest on the aforementioned loans shall not exceed 5% per annum. (13) After the wasteland reclaimed by farmers has been cultivated, the land administration authorities shall assess the land price and collect land price tax. The land price tax may be exempted for two to eight years from the date of payment. (14) These implementation measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) Foreign Minister Zhang completed his affairs in Shanghai and returned to Nanjing by train from Shanghai at 7 a.m. on the 8th. After resting briefly at his official residence, he attended the Executive Yuan meeting. In the afternoon, he received Dr. Tian Bolie, President of the World Historical Society, at the Foreign Ministry. At 8:30 p.m., he attended a banquet hosted by the French Ambassador Nazia. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

Ice in Tianjin's Hai River Thaws 15

(Tianjin) The ice in the Hai River was congested, and the lower reaches of the river channel in the Gegu and Chentangzhuang area were heavily frozen, with ice thickness of about one foot. The traffic on the Tianjin-Tanggu section was once obstructed from the 4th to the 6th. More than 20 passenger and cargo ships were blocked. The section from Tanggu to Dagu and outside Dagu Port was free of ice floes, and ships could travel freely. From 8 a.m. on the 7th, the climate and wind direction changed, and the ice gradually melted. Large ships could pass, but small ships were still obstructed. Rumors that Tangda suffered ice disasters are inaccurate. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) The shipping industry here recently received a telegram from Yingkou, stating that the weather there is getting colder, ice floes are gathering, and navigation is difficult. The port is scheduled to be closed on the 10th, and the Tianjin-Yingkou ships will stop sailing from today. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Tianjin) Ice floes were discovered outside Dagu Port on the 8th. However, as the wind turned outward, the ice floes all rolled past the port entrance. The shipping industry is now worried that if the weather turns cold and the northeast wind blows, Gukou may still be closed. The customs and the Hai River Bureau have been asked to pay attention. On the 8th, the Hai River Engineering Bureau dispatched three icebreaking ships, Kuaili, Tongling, and Feiling, and the Tianjin Shipping Company's ship Tianxing, to Gegu and outside the port to break the ice and open the waterway. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Duan Lingzhen Passes Through Nanjing and is Transported to Beiping; Government Agencies in the Capital Hold a Public Memorial Service at the Xiaguan Railway Station 18

(Nanjing) The coffin of former Chief Executive Duan was transferred from Shanghai to a special train and transported to Beiping. It arrived at Xiaguan Railway Station at 8 a.m. on the 8th. Government agencies in the capital held a public memorial service at the platform. Those present included Central Representative Ju Zheng, National Government Representative Deng Jiayan, representatives from various Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions including Weng Wenhao, Deputy Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission Feng Yuxiang, Mayor of Nanjing Ma Chaojun, as well as Cheng Qian, Bo Wenwei, He Yingqin, Shi Ying, Chen Lifu, Li Liejun, He Lian, Fang Zhi, Hong Lanyou, Shao Hua, Zhang Lisheng, Wu Siyu, Chen Jie, Shi Jingting, Gu Zhenglun, Gan Gu Pan, and more than one hundred others. In addition, the Anhui and Hefei fellow villagers associations in Nanjing sent representatives to participate in the memorial service. The National Government sent a band to the station to play music. The capital's police and gendarmerie agencies also sent police officers and gendarmerie teams to provide security. The public memorial service began at 8 a.m., presided over by Ju Zheng. After taking his place, mournful music was played. Ju Zheng, representing the central government agencies, presented flowers. Then, eulogies were read, followed by the reading of memorial texts from the Military Affairs Commission, the General Staff Headquarters, the Nanjing Municipal Government, the Anhui Fellow Villagers Association, and the Hefei Fellow Villagers Association. After the readings, everyone observed a moment of silence, and then bowed to the coffin. Duan's family prostrated themselves to express their gratitude. The music was played at 8:45 a.m. and the ceremony concluded. The hearse then crossed the river and was transported to Beiping via Pukou. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) The memorial text from the Central National Government and the various Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions to Duan (Qirui) reads: "On this eighth day of December in the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, Ju Zheng, Representative of the Central Party Department, Deng Jiayan, Representative of the National Government, and Weng Wenhao, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, offer incense and flowers to the spirit of Interim Chief Executive Duan. Your merits shone brightly for the Party and the nation. As your spirit returns to the tail of the constellation, we uphold the ancient rites to adorn your final journey and elevate the high standards of a state funeral. Now, as the hearse travels through the capital, we respectfully offer incense to express our sorrow. Gazing at the plain hearse, we remember your contribution to the restoration, and your great achievements will be recorded forever in the annals of history. May your spirit not be obscured, and come to accept our offerings. Respectfully we inform you." (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Nanjing) The memorial text from the Military Affairs Commission to Duan Qirui reads: "On this eighth day of December in the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, Chiang Chung-cheng, Chairman of the National Government Military Affairs Commission, and Vice Chairman Feng Yuxiang, leading all officers, respectfully offer incense and food to the spirit of the late Chief Executive Duan Gong Zhiquan. We say: You cultivated virtue, and were a pillar of the nation. You descended from the Song Mountain, and were born into this world at a time of great need. You built our nation, and experienced many hardships. You bore heavy responsibilities and achieved great things. You did not compete with others, and were not aware of your own greatness. Your reputation was like the East Mountain, and your name was as bright as the Big Dipper. From the past, you showed the way. You were a respected elder. In this time of difficulty, the nation is like a stormy sea. Heaven does not pity us, and has taken away a wise man. Your achievements are different from Wu, and you descend upon the Han capital. Your spirit rides on the constellation, and all mourn the loss. We rely on your spirit to be as bright as the sun and moon, and to accept this offering. Alas, we grieve! May you enjoy." (Central News Agency Dispatch, 8th)

(Xuzhou) Duan's hearse arrived in Xuzhou at 11:14 tonight. The military and police lined up to welcome it. Deputy Division Commander Huang Zuxun, along with representatives from all walks of life and Duan's students and former officials such as Ma Hechou, held a public memorial service. The train stopped for 16 minutes and then departed north. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

The Course of Events Surrounding the Murder of the Manager of the Xuchang Tobacco Company 23

(Hankou) Today, further details about the murder of Mr. Newsom, the American advisor to the Chinese government and manager of the Xuchang Tobacco Company, were received here. It is said that around 6 p.m. on Thursday evening, four bandits broke into the company's cashier's office and opened fire, wounding one staff member and one guard. Mr. Newsom went out to see what was happening, and the bandits shot him from behind. The bullet entered from his right shoulder and exited from the left side of his neck. The bandits took all the cash on hand, totaling 4,000 yuan, and fled. The police arrived, but the bandits had already escaped. Mr. Newsom was unable to move his limbs after being shot, but he remained conscious. He died at 9:20 p.m. (Reuters Dispatch, 8th)

The Corpse of a U.S. Sailor Examined by the Court 24

(Xiamen) Eric, a sailor from the U.S. ship Tulsa, went missing after landing on the 30th. His body was found on the beach of Gulangyu on the 6th. There were three wounds on his head. There were 37 U.S. dollars in his pocket. The Public Security Bureau and the court boarded the ship for investigation on the 7th and 8th. The results were not released and the newspapers were advised to be cautious in their reporting. It is unclear whether he drowned accidentally or was murdered. However, it can be known that it was not robbery. It is heard that the examination did not show knife wounds, but rather abrasions, suggesting that he fell into the water after drinking. (Special Dispatch, 8th)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Implementation of the New Soviet Constitution 42

— Lang

The new Soviet Constitution, which contains a strong democratic color, was revised and adopted by the Eighth All-Union Congress on the fifth and implemented on the same day. The content of this new constitution is not only very different from the previous one, but also better demonstrates the success of Soviet social construction. The original current Soviet Constitution was made under the environment after the revolution, and because of the victory of social construction in the past ten years, the environment has been completely different. Therefore, the old constitution is no longer applicable. Therefore, the proposal to amend the Federal Constitution was put forward at the Seventh Soviet Congress held at the end of January last year. After passing, Stalin and 30 others were appointed to form a constitutional amendment committee to engage in constitutional amendment work. After more than a year of work, it was completed in May this year and the draft was published on June 12 to seek criticism from all parties. At the end of last month, the Eighth Soviet Congress was convened to discuss the draft. After some revisions, it was fully adopted on the 5th and put into effect on the same day.

There are many characteristics of the new constitution, the most important of which is the tendency of democratization. The famous French writer Romain Rolland once said, "The new Soviet Constitution is enough to show the breadth of the meaning of democratic politics. The establishment of this new constitution shows the true meaning of freedom and equality." The most able to express the tendency of democracy is that the new constitution stipulates that the representatives of the Soviet of all levels are elected by voters in accordance with the universal, equal, direct and secret voting method. Such a thorough democratic color cannot be found in any democratic country. The adoption of this thorough democratization election law cancels many previous restrictions on the people's elections and expands the scope of the right to vote. This cannot but be said to be the success of Soviet social construction.

The second is the provision on private property. Since the adoption of the New Economic Policy in the Soviet Union, private capital has been allowed to exist. This new constitution expressly stipulates the legal protection of private property. The draft constitution did not stipulate the right to inherit citizens' personal property, but it was revised in this congress, stipulating that the right of inheritance is protected by law. In this way, the new constitution is more obvious in protecting private economy. However, we must recognize that this kind of private economy is "limited to being based on individual labor without exploiting the labor of others."

The third is the provision on declaring war. Article 49 of the new constitution stipulates that "During the adjournment of the Supreme Soviet of the Soviet Union, if the Soviet Union is subjected to armed attack or if it is necessary to perform the obligations of international mutual assistance to resist aggression, the Presidium shall declare war." The third sentence in this article was not in the constitutional draft, but was added in this congress. Because after the conclusion of the French-Soviet Mutual Assistance Agreement, even if the Soviet Union itself is not subjected to armed attack, but France is subjected to an unprovoked attack, the Soviet Union also has the obligation to declare war. This treaty provision is obviously aimed at countries such as Germany and Japan that are invading outwards.

In addition, there are certainly many characteristics of the new Soviet constitution, which will not be listed here. In short, the making of this new constitution is really the fruit of the successful social construction of the Soviet Union in the past ten years. The implementation of this democratic new constitution not only has great significance internally, but also has a great effect externally. Because in this world filled with fascist forces, democratic politics has become the end of its rope, but now such a new force has been added. This has a great contribution to the maintenance of world peace. Moreover, the amendment of this constitution in the Soviet Union makes it easier to approach the three major democratic countries of Britain, France and the United States, forming a grand alliance of democratic countries to deal with the aggressive behavior of international fascism. This also has a very important impact on the international political situation.

The British King's Marriage Has a Sudden Turn—Mrs. Simpson Suddenly Issues a Statement, Saying She Is Willing to Retire If It Can Solve the Problem 43

(London) Although the marriage advocated by King Edward is not approved by the cabinet, the constitutional crisis caused by this matter will not necessarily require the King to abdicate. There is still room for maneuver in the current situation. (Seventh Day Shanghai Evening Post Special Dispatch)

(London) Lord Brownlow, a friend of the British King and a major landowner, read a statement issued by Mrs. Simpson to dozens of reporters at the Grand Hotel in Cannes, France, last night. He then handed over the original manuscript to everyone present and solemnly stated that Mrs. Simpson had not received any visitors. The statement was signed by Mrs. Simpson, but Mrs. Simpson did not attend. It said, "In the past few weeks, Mrs. Simpson has repeatedly tried to avoid any actions or suggestions that would be detrimental to the British King or his throne. Her attitude has not changed. If she withdraws now and can solve the problem, then she is willing to withdraw from this unpleasant situation that cannot be sustained by both parties." This statement came suddenly, and even the palace staff were surprised when they heard it. They did not expect Mrs. Simpson to have such a firm position. Even the British King's entourage at Belvedere Palace did not know about it at first. However, this statement cannot end the current crisis, but is only Mrs. Simpson's personal opinion. The phrase "If she withdraws now and can solve the problem" is particularly noteworthy. According to insiders, Mrs. Simpson's move was purely her own decision. Now only the British King's actions can end the current situation. No matter how important other steps are, their effectiveness is limited. However, Mrs. Simpson's move has aroused a more hopeful atmosphere in Parliament. People generally believe that this is also a way out of the difficulty. Others believe that this move may lead to a sudden turn in the situation. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

(New York) Lord Brownlow, who escorted Mrs. Simpson to France, spoke with a reporter from the American News Agency on the phone in Cannes, France, today, saying, "The statement issued by Mrs. Simpson shows that if her withdrawal can completely solve the current difficulties, then Mrs. Simpson will definitely withdraw immediately. Therefore, Mrs. Simpson's attitude is clear. Now Mrs. Simpson is very tired and does not want to be disturbed by others." Brownlow refused to indicate whether Mrs. Simpson's statement meant that she had actually withdrawn, but said that everything should be decided by the British King. The reporter then asked what relationship the British King's abdication had with Mrs. Simpson's plan. Brownlow said that Mrs. Simpson had not discussed this matter with him. The reporter asked again, "When will they get married?" The Lord said, "How strange this question is! How would I know?" (Seventh Day National News Dispatch)

(London) British official circles declared today that the statement issued by Sir Brownlow on behalf of Mrs. Simpson in Cannes, France, must have been done at the will of the British King. From this, it can be seen that the British King may have decided not to marry for the time being. (Seventh Day National News Dispatch)

Cannes, France The Associated Press learned from reliable sources today that some of the wording in Mrs. Simpson's statement was actually instructed by a certain party in London via wireless telephone. (Eighth Day National News Dispatch)

(Washington) The Washington Evening Star carried today that before Mrs. Simpson went to Cannes, France, from England, she told the British King that if the King's decision affected his responsibility to the Empire, he should not be troubled by his obligations to her. According to the owner of the Evening Star, who has family ties with Mrs. Simpson, this news is accurate and reliable. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

A Mysterious Airplane Flies from England to Southern France—The Names of the Three People on Board Are Unknown—Presumably Flying to Mrs. Simpson's Location 44

(London) Today, a special airplane departed from Lawton Airport, destination unknown. There were three people on board, and their names are also unknown. It is said that they are government officials. (Eighth Day National News Dispatch)

(London) This morning, a mysterious airplane departed from Gatwick, England, and flew to Cannes, France, via Croydon (near London), Poilloux (near Paris), and Lyon. The airplane was a biplane and belonged to British Airways. When it landed at Croydon Airport, three passengers suddenly boarded the airplane, but even the airline did not know their names. The airplane arrived in Lyon at 2:15 PM and continued to take off at 3:00 PM, heading towards Cannes. (Eighth Day Havas Dispatch)

(London) There is much speculation about the mysterious airplane that flew from Croydon Airport to Cannes, France, this morning. The airplane stopped at Le Bourget Airport in France for more than an hour due to bad weather. Seeing that there was no hope of stopping the wind and rain for a while, it continued to take off after refueling. It is said that there were three men on board. Another saying is that these three people are from the British Home Office. A team of gendarmes guarded the Lyon Airport, where the airplane was scheduled to land for refueling, and all idlers were not allowed to approach the airport. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The News Chronicle published a commentary on Mrs. Simpson's statement today, saying, "The King's personal abandonment of the path to marriage has now been clarified by a word from his lover. What she can do, he can also do, and it is his duty." (Seventh Day National News Dispatch)

(London) The Evening Standard reported that Mrs. Simpson not only has a responsibility to her lover, but also to the King of England. Now that Mrs. Simpson has issued a statement, unwilling to put the British King in a difficult situation because of her, the British King should be able to prioritize the country and no longer be persistent. The Daily Express said that Mrs. Simpson's statement can only be regarded as a declaration. The Morning Post carried that whatever final decision the British King makes will inevitably make him unhappy, which is a natural trend. Although the article published by Mrs. Simpson may be able to save the most deteriorated situation, it is enough to prove the above point. If the British King can resolutely sacrifice private feelings and take the right path, then his current pain will be richly rewarded in his future peaceful heart and the general trend of the world. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

The British King's Palace is Lit Up All Night Long—The Duke of York and Baldwin are Busy Traveling Between the Palace and the Prime Minister's Residence 45

(London) Prime Minister Baldwin and Monkton, Legal Advisor of Cornwall, both set off for Bielvittier Palace at 4:15 PM today. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Belvedere Palace was still brightly lit until dawn today. The Duke of York went to see the British King last night and left late at night, returning to his residence in Windsor. The Duke of York is currently residing with Monkton, Legal Advisor of Cornwall. The Duke of York returned to Belvedere Palace again after midnight and stayed there overnight. At about 9:00 AM this morning, he also came to London with Sir Peacock, Receiver General of Cornwall. There was no activity at Downing Street Prime Minister's Residence this morning. Only Home Secretary Simon and First Lord of the Admiralty Hoare went to see Prime Minister Baldwin. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The Attorney General of Cornwall, namely the King's confidant Monkton, went to the Prime Minister's Office at 10:15 AM today and held talks with Prime Minister Baldwin for two and a half hours before leaving and returning to the Belvedere Palace in the evening to meet with the King to report. Prime Minister Baldwin arrived at his official residence at 9:15 PM. Half an hour later, a royal car drove to the residence, and two people got out of the car and went inside. Who they were is unknown. At 10:30 PM, the car of the King's younger brother, the Duke of York, arrived at Belvedere Palace. It is not known whether there was anyone in the car. Several fascists gathered near Buckingham Palace in the evening to hold a demonstration, which was eventually dispersed by the police. (Seventh Day Havas Dispatch)

(London) People from all over the British Empire expressed their support for King Edward's marriage today. However, according to powerful sources, Edward will ultimately not be able to have both beauty and country. It is rumored that the cabinet has passed a draft abdication edict and presented it to the King for his perusal. The King is considering flying to Cannes, France, to discuss with Mrs. Simpson, but it is not certain whether his entourage will allow him to do so. Labour MP Wegwood, a leader who advocates supporting the King, told the press after Prime Minister Baldwin's speech in the House of Commons today, "The current situation has improved slightly. The cabinet will not take any action before the King replies. I really don't understand why the King needs to abdicate. Last Saturday, we all thought that the abdication issue was imminent, but until now, the emotions of the people have gradually changed, and the King does not need to make a decision in a hurry. The government should know the danger of the rise of fascism. The Fascist Party has taken the opportunity to express that they are the King's only supporters. This situation is quite dangerous." (Seventh Day National News Dispatch)

(London) The situation regarding the marriage issue has not changed this morning. The Attorney General of Cornwall, namely the King's confidant Monkton, and the Revenue Director of the county, Peacock, went to the Downing Street Prime Minister's Office yesterday to meet with Prime Minister Baldwin. This morning, at 9:00 AM, they returned to London from Belvedere Palace in the King's official car to conduct official business. This morning, a special airplane flew to Cannes, France, from Croydon Airport in the suburbs, carrying three passengers whose names are unknown. Prime Minister Baldwin received Home Secretary Sir Simon and First Lord of the Admiralty Sir Hoare at 10:45 AM. Someone invited Churchill, the leader of the extremist faction of the Conservative Party, to deliver a broadcast speech to the United States on the constitutional dispute, which Churchill immediately refused. Former Foreign Secretary Sir Austen Chamberlain and former British High Commissioner to Egypt Lord Lloyd originally planned to travel to Paris today, but they have now canceled their plans. In addition, the stock exchange has improved because of the more hopeful prospect of resolving the marriage issue. The exchange rate of the pound and the market prices of various British securities have all risen. (Eighth Day Havas Dispatch)

Members of Parliament and Cabinet Members Have Frequent Contacts—Lively Discussions in the Lounge 46

(London) When the House of Commons discussed the British King's marriage today, former cabinet member and independent MP Wegwood asked Prime Minister Baldwin if he could be given an opportunity to discuss the motion he had proposed on Thursday. (Wegwood's intention was to declare that having previously sworn allegiance to the British King, this oath would not be shaken by any form of coronation ceremony or the absence of any dignitaries at the coronation. The House of Commons would not appoint another person as the monarch of England. He asked the House of Commons to approve this motion.) The Prime Minister replied that he could not. Wegwood continued to speak, but the Speaker stopped him, saying that the Prime Minister had given a clear answer to his question. The diplomatic seats in the House of Commons today were full. Sir Miville, the private secretary of the Duke of York, the heir to the throne, was also in the audience. During the meeting, Churchill was quite eloquent. Those who supported the government said that Churchill's statement that the cabinet had no right to advise the King to abdicate and that the cabinet had no right to predetermine its position without first consulting the will of Parliament was mainly to oppose the Prime Minister. The King still holds the decision. (Seventh Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Home Secretary Sir Simon, on behalf of Prime Minister Baldwin, replied to the question of Labour opposition leader Attlee today, stating that the Prime Minister would not add anything to the declaration made yesterday. (Eighth Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) Labour MPs convened a meeting today to discuss the constitutional dispute caused by the British King's intention to marry Mrs. Simpson. The number of attendees was unprecedented, but no decision was made. It is said that the party's current opinion is that the government has the responsibility to deal with the situation. However, when the opportunity is slightly missed, the Prime Minister is afraid of being criticized by all parties. The meeting also believed that there was no need to formulate a special policy at this time. It is heard that at the meeting today, many speakers advocated that the British King should accept the advice of the cabinet when it gives its advice.

Baldwin also had informal talks with cabinet members this morning, but it seems that there will be no major developments before the British King makes a final decision. Around noon today, there was no sign that Baldwin would make a declaration in the House of Commons. At the same time, Foreign Secretary Eden has also decided not to attend the League of Nations Executive Council meeting convened in Geneva on Thursday because of this matter. The British side will be represented by diplomat Viscount Cranborne. The number of important figures coming and going has not been as large today as in the past. The Duke and Duchess of York returned to Piccadilly Residence this morning. The British King's younger brother, the Duke of Kent, drove to Bielvittier Palace in a black and white car this afternoon. (Seventh Day Reuters Dispatch)

(London) According to general claims within the House of Commons lounge, the House of Commons hopes that the King will announce his final decision before the end of this week, so that the volatile and uncertain situation will quickly disappear, and the relationship between the country and the territories of the Empire will also tend to be stable. In short, the attitude expressed by all members of Parliament has made it impossible for the King to resist on constitutional grounds. Even if the general public expresses sympathy to the King, it will be of no avail. Therefore, the general situation has not changed. As for Churchill's actions and similar fascist demonstrations, they only make members of Parliament fear that a small number of politicians will use the marriage issue to oppose Parliament or constitutional procedures, and therefore have to be vigilant. Moreover, the whole House of Commons applauded Prime Minister Baldwin this afternoon, not entirely for the Prime Minister, but also to express support for the constitutional principles represented by the Prime Minister. What is currently being discussed in the House of Commons lounge is only the question of when the King will abdicate. It is generally expected that if the King does not give up the idea of marrying Mrs. Simpson, he will announce his abdication at the end of this week. According to several people in the inner court, the King has not yet signed the abdication document, and his attitude is still hesitant.

There is also a saying in the House of Commons lounge that before making a final decision, the King will go to Cannes, France, to visit Mrs. Simpson. The official airplane is currently waiting for orders at the Belvedere Palace airport.

In addition, if the King's abdication becomes a fact, who should be the successor? There are various speculations, and opinions differ. Some Conservative Party members support the establishment of the daughter of the current King's second brother, the Duke of York, Princess Elizabeth (currently ten years old) as Queen, and the establishment of a Regency Council to administer state affairs. However, no decision has been made on this matter yet. The King's confidant, namely the Attorney General of Cornwall, Monkton, is currently negotiating with the cabinet to resolve the issue of the King's status after abdication. (Seventh Day Havas Dispatch)

Internal Changes in the Spanish Government, Two More Republicans Added, Garcia Succeeds as Foreign Minister, Preparations for a Major Battle Between the Two Armies 49

Madrid: The Madrid government has become more leftist today, appointing communist Garcia to succeed Faber as Minister of Foreign Affairs. Garcia's original position as Chairman of the Military Commission has also been succeeded by another communist, Anton. (National Telegram, 7th)

Madrid: The Nationalist army artillery resumed bombarding the capital around midnight yesterday. Several large shells fell on the main street and near the British Embassy. A large-scale new attack on the capital by General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the Nationalist army, is expected at any moment. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Madrid: Twenty-three Nationalist army bombers recently flew in formation to the city of Guadalajara, northeast of Madrid, and carried out bombing raids. Most of the bombs dropped were incendiary bombs, which completely destroyed the Duke of Infantado's residence in the city. Many other houses, especially the hospitals, also suffered heavy losses. More than twenty residents were killed in the bombing, and many women and children were injured. (Havas Agency dispatch, 8th)

Madrid: Nationalist army aircraft reappeared over the capital today to take photos of the defenses, but did not drop bombs. The two armies are now preparing for a decisive battle, and the outbreak is not far away. However, the Basque army in Santander and Bilbao and the government army on the Ebro River have had to temporarily suspend their attacks due to the snow. (National Telegram, 7th)

Madrid: The battle situation on the front lines around Madrid has been very quiet in recent days. Generally speaking, the Nationalist army has received reinforcements in the past two days, so they are actively deploying their positions, preparing for a large-scale offensive at any moment to determine the final victory or defeat. On the government army's side, they are also preparing to resist. The militia units are now reinforcing the positions they have recently captured, and are building defensive fortifications around the capital. It is generally expected that the Nationalist army will launch an offensive tomorrow, but it is not yet known where they will attack. Some people believe that the two towns of Pozuelo and Humera in the northern suburbs are more likely to be attacked. The city authorities have been actively stockpiling various major food supplies in recent days. Two hundred trucks a day are transporting food to the capital. After unloading the goods, they are fully loaded with residents and head to the Autonomous Region of Catalonia and the eastern coastal provinces to avoid the disaster. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Valencia: Recently, 525 Spaniards in Madrid, most of whom were members of the fascist Falange party, sought refuge in the Finnish Embassy. The authorities learned of this and immediately entered the embassy to arrest them. Foreign Minister Alvarez has sent a telegram to the Finnish government protesting against the Finnish ambassador's sheltering of fascist figures and demanding that the ambassador be replaced immediately. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(London) The Non-Intervention Committee on the Spanish Civil War is now scheduled to hold a plenary session tomorrow to discuss the issue of foreign volunteers serving in Spain. The sub-committee of the Non-Intervention Committee has recently drafted a report on this issue, which is ready to be submitted to the Non-Intervention Committee for review. The content of the report can be divided into two points: (1) The sub-committee unanimously believes that all acts of intervention in the Spanish Civil War, whether direct or indirect, should be prohibited. (2) It is advocated that the recruitment, departure, and transit of volunteers should be prohibited. Finally, the report asks the Non-Intervention Committee to request the governments of all relevant countries to submit to the committee the measures they intend to take to prohibit volunteers from serving in Spain for review. Regarding the first point, the Soviet representative also accepted it, but on the condition that other countries accept the second point. As for the representatives of Germany, Italy, and Portugal, they have not yet received instructions from their respective governments regarding the second point, so they have not expressed their position. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

German Foreign Minister Explains the German-Japanese Agreement Is Not Against China 58

Former Chairman of the Far East Study Group Speaks on Sino-German Trade Relations

(Berlin) Chinese Ambassador to Germany Cheng Tianfang recently visited Foreign Minister Neurath and inquired about the anti-communist agreement signed by Germany and Japan. Neurath confirmed the declaration recently issued in Nanjing by the German Ambassador to China, Doddmann, saying that the German-Japanese anti-communist agreement is not directed against China, nor is it a tool to promote Japanese oppression in northern China. As for the standing committee established in the agreement, its scope of activities is limited to Germany and Japan. In addition, some Chinese students here expressed concern about the consequences of the rapprochement between Germany and Japan. Ambassador Cheng Tianfang earnestly persuaded them to remain calm and abide by discipline. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(Berlin) Former Chairman of the Far East Study Group, that is, Plenipotentiary Minister Kerp, gave a speech at the Far East Association yesterday afternoon entitled "New China." Chinese Ambassador Cheng Tianfang and senior officials of the embassy attended. Since the German-Japanese "anti-communist" agreement has just been concluded, Kerp's speech has aroused great interest. Kerp said, "The German study group's trip to the Far East was to study the markets of Asian countries, especially the Chinese market, to what extent they can be expanded. By referring to the commercial policies in Germany's new economic plan, we can promote mutual trade. The Chinese reconstruction plan, especially the military organization, is very important and has been very effective. The Chinese National Government and the Kuomintang have the same goals, and their actions are like arms and fingers working together. Regarding the cooperation between China and other countries and the League of Nations, the industrial relations maintained by Britain, the United States, and Germany are closer than those of other countries. Germany has been supplying China with large quantities of goods in recent years. In terms of financial relations, Britain and the United States occupy a more advantageous position in China. In conclusion, Germany's friendship with China is very sincere. Germany can supply all the industrial products needed for China's reconstruction without limitation. China is rich in natural resources and can supply Germany with various raw materials, the quantity of which may be larger than the industrial products supplied by Germany." (Havas dispatch, 8th)

Russian Ship Discovered in Hokkaido, Japanese People Make a Fuss 59

Because the "Four Strong" and "Typina" incidents had occurred successively before, the Foreign Affairs Section of the Hokkaido Government attached great importance to it, and requested the Ominato Naval Base to send aircraft and destroyers.
